commit 3a308f3903347949cab8559da370ae97985b5b8b
Author: Andrea Vacondio <andrea.vacondio@gmail.com>
Date:   Wed Jun 4 11:29:26 2014 +0200

    Validation on Enter key made optional.
    
    validate method doesn't make the validation state NOT_VALIDATED prior to
    validation. NOT_VALIDATED state is set only when text of the field
    changes. This avoid to trigger a VALID-NOT_VALIDATED-VALID chain every
    time the validate() method is called which was in practice triggering
    the state change listeners everytime the validate() was called, even if
    the state wasn't actually changed.
